;
proc sort data=interval;
by Year site;
run;
proc print; run;

proc means data=interval;
class year site date trt rep;
variable incidence;
output out=out1 mean=incidence std=stdev;
run;
proc print data=out1;
where _type_=31;
run;
proc sort data=out1;
where _type_=31;
by Year Site;
run;

proc sort data=interval;
by Year site;
run;

proc glimmix plots=residualpanel maxopt=500 data=interval;
tincidence=log10(incidence+1);;
where Year=2020 and site='Prosser'; 
class date trt rep;
model tincidence=trt|date/ddfm=kr dist=normal;
random rep;
random _residual_/sub=rep*trt type=ar(1);
lsmeans trt|date/lines;
run;

proc glimmix plots=residualpanel maxopt=500 data=interval;
tincidence=log10(incidence+1);;
where Year=2020 and site='Toppenis'; 
class date trt rep;
model tincidence=trt|date/ddfm=kr dist=normal;
random trt*rep;
random _residual_/sub=rep*trt type=ar(1);
lsmeans trt|date/lines slicediff=date;
run;

proc glimmix plots=residualpanel maxopt=500 data=interval;
tincidence=log10(incidence+1);
where Year=2021 and site='Prosser';
class date trt rep;
model tincidence=trt|date/ddfm=kr dist=normal;
random rep*trt;
random _residual_/sub=rep*trt type=ar(1);
lsmeans trt|date/lines;
run;

proc glimmix plots=residualpanel maxopt=500 data=interval;
tincidence=log10(incidence+1);
where Year=2021 and site='Toppenis';
class date trt rep;
model tincidence=trt|date/ddfm=kr dist=normal;
*random rep rep*trt; 
random _residual_/sub=rep*trt type=ar(1);
lsmeans trt|date/lines slicediff=date;;
run;

proc glimmix plots=residualpanel maxopt=500 data=interval;
tincidence=log10(incidence+1);
where Year=2022 and site='Prosser';
class date trt rep;
model tincidence=trt|date/ddfm=kr dist=normal;
random rep*trt rep;
random _residual_/sub=rep*trt type=ar(1);
lsmeans trt|date/lines;
run;

tincidence=log10(incidence+1);
where Year=2022 and site='Toppenis';
